<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вознамериться.html>вознаме́риться</a> (15611)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наме́р-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">namér-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознамериться.html>вознаме́риться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznaméritʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вознаме́риваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to intend (+ to), to make up one's mind (+ to), to conceive the idea <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вознамериться.html>вознаме́рился</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>voznamérilsja</b> ujéxatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he took it into his head to leave</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вознамериться.html>вознаме́рились</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осчастливить.html>осчастли́вить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>voznamérilisʹ</b> vsex osčastlívitʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they conceived the idea of making everyone happy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***вознесение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вознесение.html>вознесе́ние</a> (25944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вознес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознесение.html>вознесе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznesénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознесение.html>вознесе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознесение.html>вознесе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознесение.html>вознесе́ний</a></b>)
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознести.html>вознести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознестись.html>вознести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возноситься.html>возноси́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li>to rise, to tower

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become conceited/stuck-up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознести.html>вознести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***возникать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ть</a> (1000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ВъзникнѪти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">VŭzniknǪti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznikátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникнуть.html>возни́кнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arise, to appear, to emerge, to originate, to spring up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>При</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́гут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проблема.html>пробле́мы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pri rešénii dánnoj zadáči mógut <b>voznikátʹ</b> nékotoryje problémy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">While solving the given task a few problems can <b>arise</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to object, to protest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>иди́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́й</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Idí i ne <b>voznikáj</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(Just) <b>shut up</b> and go.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***возникнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возникнуть.html>возни́кнуть</a> (940)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ВъзникнѪти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">VŭzniknǪti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникнуть.html>возни́кнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozníknutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возникать.html>возника́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arise, to appear, to emerge, to originate, to spring up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>При</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:данный.html>да́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задача.html>зада́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возникнуть.html>возни́кли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:проблема.html>пробле́мы</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pri rešénii dánnoj zadáči u nevó <b>vozníkli</b> nékotoryje problémy.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">While solving the given task a few problems have <b>arisen</b> for him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***возносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a> (23763)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознести.html>вознести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to raise high, to uplift</li>
<li>to exalt
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небе́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voznosítʹ</b> do nebés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to praise to the skies</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́тву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voznosítʹ</b> molítvu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">To offer up a prayer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хвала.html>хвалу́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voznosítʹ</b> xvalú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to praise; eulogize</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небеса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voznosítʹ</b> na nebesá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">take to heaven</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возноситься.html>возноси́ться</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voznosítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознестись.html>вознести́сь</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">voznestísʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возноситься.html>возноси́ться</a> (26639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возноситься.html>возноси́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznosítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вознестись.html>вознести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rise, to tower
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возноситься.html>возноси́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:небо.html>небеса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>voznosítʹsja</b> na nebesá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ascend to heaven</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ironical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become conceited/stuck-up</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возносить.html>возноси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voznosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***возня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возня́</a> (7634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a>(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ня́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возня́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">voznjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возни́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возни́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fuss, bustle, scurrying, fumbling
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1935</b>,  Владимир Владимирович Набоков (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vladimir_Nabokov" class="extiw" title="w:Vladimir Nabokov">Vladimir Vladimirovich Nabokov</a>),  chapter 1, in Dmitri Nabokov, transl., <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:приглашение.html>Приглаше́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:казнь.html>казнь</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Invitation_to_a_Beheading" class="extiw" title="w:Invitation to a Beheading">Invitation to a Beheading</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тюремщик.html>тюре́мщик</a> родио́н <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отпирать.html>отпира́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>дверь</a> цинцинна́товой <a href = vnd.unilang:камера.html>ка́меры</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a>, — <a href = vnd.unilang:всегдашний.html>всегда́шняя</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возня.html>возня́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:дверь.html>Дверь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наконец.html>наконе́ц</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уступить.html>уступи́ла</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tjurémščik Rodión dólgo otpirál dverʹ Cincinnátovoj kámery, — ne tot ključ, — vsegdášnjaja <b>voznjá</b>. Dverʹ nakonéc ustupíla.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Rodion, the jailer, took a long time to unlock the door of Cincinnatus’ cell — it was the wrong key — and there was the usual <b>fuss</b>. At last the door yielded.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>trouble, bother
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  Андрей Юрьевич <a href = vnd.unilang:курок.html>Курко́в</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrey_Kurkov" class="extiw" title="w:Andrey Kurkov">Andrey Yuryevich Kurkov</a>),  chapter 1, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:игра.html>Игра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отрезанный.html>отре́занный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палец.html>палец</a></cite>  | <cite>The Case of the General's Thumb</cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>Ни́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:действительно.html>действи́тельно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нуждаться.html>нужда́лся</a> <a href = ***возобновить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a> (15266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">воз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">voz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обновить.html>обнови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozobnovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to renew, to resume, to recommence, to revive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:абонемент.html>абонеме́нт</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>догово́р</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovítʹ</b> abonemént (dogovór)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to renew a subscription (an agreement)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovítʹ</b> zanjátija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resume/recommence lessons</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломатический.html>дипломати́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovítʹ</b> diplomatíčeskije otnošénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resume diplomatic relations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:переговоры.html>перегово́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovítʹ</b> peregovóry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reopen/resume negotiations/talks/discussions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***возобновлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a> (28174)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozobnovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozobnovljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновить.html>возобнови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to renew, to resume, to recommence, to revive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:абонемент.html>абонеме́нт</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:договор.html>догово́р</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovljátʹ</b> abonemént (dogovór)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to renew a subscription (an agreement)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovljátʹ</b> zanjátija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resume/recommence lessons</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дипломатический.html>дипломати́ческие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отношение.html>отноше́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovljátʹ</b> diplomatíčeskije otnošénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to resume diplomatic relations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возобновлять.html>возобновля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:переговоры.html>перегово́ры</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozobnovljátʹ</b> peregovóry</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reopen/resume negotiations/talks/discussions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***возомнить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возомнить.html>возомни́ть</a> (19893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">возо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мнить.html>мнить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mnitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возомнить.html>возомни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozomnítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to imagine, to suspect</li>
<li>to think too high (of oneself)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:возомнить.html>возомни́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:эксперт.html>экспе́ртом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vozomnítʹ</b> sebjá ekspértom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to consider oneself an expert (mistakenly)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возопивший.html>возопи́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozopívšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возопить.html>возопи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozopítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<table style="float:right; clear:right; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" width="210" class="morfotable ru">

***возопить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возопить.html>возопи́ть</a> (18751)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возопить.html>возопи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozopítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вопия́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопить.html>вопи́ть</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ть</a> (2684)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возразить.html>возрази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vozražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возразить.html>возрази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to object, to mind, to protest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:возражать.html>возража́ете</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пригласить.html>приглашу́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понятый.html>поняты́х</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli vy ne <b>vozražájete</b>, ja priglašú ponjatýx.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If you don't <b>mind</b>, I'll invite the witnesses.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
